# Dean's List Honors 1144, Reveals Registrar
## 
### 
Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.
A breakdown of the total re
peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.

istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.

peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.
A breakdown of the total re
peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.

peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.
A breakdown of the total re
peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.
A breakdown of the total re
peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.
A breakdown of the total re
peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.
A breakdown of the total re
peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.

peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.

peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.

peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.

peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.

peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.
A breakdown of the total re
peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.
A breakdown of the total re
peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.

Dr. Harvey Hall, Registrar, re
cently released ihe names of 1144
men and women students who
were able to tally the 3.20 grade
point average necessary to make
, the Dean's List.
Only students who were reg
istered for three quarters out of
the past four will be found on
the list; qualifying members of
the class of 1966 were honored
at the graduation ceremonies
last June.
A breakdown of the total re
peals that 752 men and 392 wom
en made the grade.
